DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.25
  ARG PARALLELISM=96
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y protobuf-compiler
  RUN go install github.com/mgechev/revive@latest \
      && go install honnef.co/go/tools/cmd/staticcheck@latest \
      && go install -v google.golang.org/protobuf/cmd/protoc-gen-go@latest \
      && go install -v -buildvcs=false google.golang.org/grpc/cmd/protoc-gen-go-grpc@latest
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy -go=1.25 && go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}
  RUN cd examples && go mod tidy -go=1.25 -compat=1.25 && go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}
  RUN cd gcp/observability && go mod tidy -go=1.25 && go mod verify
  RUN find . -name go.mod -execdir sh -c 'go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}' \;
  RUN go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} ./...
  RUN cd examples && go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} ./...
  RUN go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} google.golang.org/grpc/cmd/protoc-gen-go-grpc
  RUN protoc --go-grpc_out=. --go_out=. -I. path/to/protos
  RUN revive -cpu_count ${PARALLELISM} -config revive.toml ./...
  RUN staticcheck -checks=all -parallel ${PARALLELISM} ./...
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.25
  ARG PARALLELISM=96
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y protobuf-compiler
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy -go=1.25
  RUN go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}
  RUN cd examples && go mod tidy -go=1.25 -compat=1.25
  RUN cd examples && go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}
  RUN cd gcp/observability && go mod tidy -go=1.25 && go mod verify
  RUN find . -name go.mod -execdir sh -c 'go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}' \;
  RUN go install github.com/mgechev/revive@latest \
      && go install honnef.co/go/tools/cmd/staticcheck@latest \
      && go install -v google.golang.org/protobuf/cmd/protoc-gen-go@latest \
      && go install -v -buildvcs=false google.golang.org/grpc/cmd/protoc-gen-go-grpc@latest
  RUN go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} ./...
  RUN cd examples && go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} ./...
  RUN go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} google.golang.org/grpc/cmd/protoc-gen-go-grpc
  RUN protoc --go-grpc_out=. --go_out=. -I. path/to/protos
  RUN revive -cpu_count ${PARALLELISM} -config scripts/revive.toml ./...
  RUN staticcheck -checks=all -parallel ${PARALLELISM} ./...
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:

  ARG PARALLELISM=96
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y protobuf-compiler
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy -go=1.25
  RUN go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}
  RUN cd examples && go mod tidy -go=1.25 -compat=1.25 && go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}
  RUN cd gcp/observability && go mod tidy -go=1.25 && go mod verify
  RUN find . -name go.mod -execdir sh -c 'go mod vendor -v -parallel=${PARALLELISM}' \;
  RUN go install github.com/mgechev/revive@latest \
      && go install honnef.co/go/tools/cmd/staticcheck@latest \
      && go install -v google.golang.org/protobuf/cmd/protoc-gen-go@latest \
      && go install -v -buildvcs=false google.golang.org/grpc/cmd/protoc-gen-go-grpc@latest
  RUN go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} ./...
  RUN cd examples && go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} ./...
  RUN go build -v -p=${PARALLELISM} google.golang.org/grpc/cmd/protoc-gen-go-grpc
  RUN protoc --go-grpc_out=. --go_out=. -I. path/to/protos
  RUN revive -cpu_count ${PARALLELISM} -config scripts/revive.toml ./...
  RUN staticcheck -checks=all -parallel ${PARALLELISM} ./...
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
